[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*It matters which side we choose. Even if there will never be more light than darkness. Even if there can be no more joy in the galaxy than there is pain. For every action we undertake, for every word we speak, for every life we touch, it matters. I don't turn toward the light because it means someday I'll win some sort of cosmic game. I turn toward it because it is the light.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

**Qui-Gon Jinn**, a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender"), was a venerable if maverick [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") who lived during the last [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"). He was a wise and well-respected member of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), and was offered a seat on the [Jedi Council](/wiki/Jedi_Council "Jedi Council"), but chose to reject and follow his own path. Adhering to a philosophy centered around the [Living Force](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force"), Jinn strove to follow the will of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") even when his actions conflicted with the wishes of the High [Council](/wiki/Jedi_Council "Jedi Council"). After encountering [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), Jinn brought him to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), convinced he had found the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"). His [dying](/wiki/Death "Death") wish was for Skywalker to become a [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and ultimately restore balance to the Force.

[Born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") on the [Core World](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") Coruscant, the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") around [80 BBY](/wiki/80_BBY "80 BBY"), Jinn learned the ways of the Force as the [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") before ultimately attaining the rank of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") in around [58 BBY](/wiki/58_BBY "58 BBY"). In [44 BBY](/wiki/44_BBY "44 BBY") he would go on to take an apprentice of his own, [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), who adhered to the principles of the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") more than his own master. Although their relationship was sometimes tough, the two Jedi overcame early difficulties during a [mission to Pijal](/wiki/Mission_to_Pijal "Mission to Pijal"), which concluded in Jinn turning down a request to join the Jedi Council to continue teaching his apprentice. When the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") initiated a [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") of the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"), Jinn and Kenobi were [dispatched](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Saak%27ak "Escape from the Saak'ak") to resolve the crisis at the request of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum"). Influenced by the mysterious [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), the Federation launched a full-scale [invasion](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") of Naboo, forcing the Jedi to rescue [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") after the fall of [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed").

During their journey to the [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") capital, the group was forced to land on the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") planet [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") where Jinn encountered a young [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") named Anakin Skywalker. Using a scientific method to gauge the boy's potential, he learned that Skywalker had more [midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian") in his [blood](/wiki/DNA "DNA") than any Force-sensitive in [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"), including [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"). The revelation that he was the result of a miracle birth—a child born of a [mother](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars"), but had no [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent")—confirmed Jinn's suspicion that Skywalker was the Chosen One destined to restore balance to the Force. Before departing the [desert](/wiki/Desert "Desert") world with Skywalker, Jinn was confronted by Sidious' [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"). Although their [duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Tatooine "Duel on Tatooine") was brief, it convinced Jinn that the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") had returned after a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") of silence.

At the [Temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple"), Jinn was adamant that Skywalker was the Chosen One and should, therefore, be inducted into the Jedi Order. However, having inspected Skywalker for themselves, the High Council deemed him too old, emotional, and dangerously full of fear and anger. Jinn saw their decision as a temporary setback, but the need to resolve the situation on [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") Amidala's [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") forced him to set aside his plans for Skywalker. During the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), Jinn and Kenobi confronted [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Maul together. While they initially managed to fend off the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord")'s attacks, master and apprentice were eventually separated during the [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel"), resulting in Jinn sustaining a mortal injury. Rushing to his master's aid, Kenobi fought and ultimately defeated the [Dathomirian](/wiki/Dathomirian "Dathomirian") Sith, but could not save Jinn. With his last breath, Jinn made Kenobi promise that he would take Skywalker as his apprentice. Having secured Kenobi's word, Jinn became [one with the Force](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"), dying with the certainty that he had found the prophesied Chosen One.

## Biography[]

### Early life[]

:   "*Qui-Gon Jinn would never join you.*"  
    "*Don't be so sure, my young Jedi. You forget that he was once my apprentice, just as you were once his.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Count Dooku[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_II-12)

 [![Count Dooku, Jinn's former master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Jedi-Dooku-Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20210802232644) [![Count Dooku, Jinn's former master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Jedi-Dooku-Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20210802232644)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Jedi-Dooku-Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20210802232644) 

Count Dooku, Jinn's former master.

 

Qui-Gon Jinn was a [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") on the [galactic](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant")[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate-1) circa [80 BBY](/wiki/80_BBY "80 BBY").[[2]](#cite_note-Date_80BBY-2) He was taken to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") as a boy[[14]](#cite_note-JMM1-14) for [training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") by the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and was assigned to the [Heliost Clan](/wiki/Heliost_Clan "Heliost Clan") where he learned [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat") from [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Tera Sinube](/wiki/Tera_Sinube "Tera Sinube").[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

When Jinn was twelve years old, he was assigned as a [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") to Jedi Master [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), from whom he learned the ways of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force").[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate-1)[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_II-12) He'd spent his last night in the younglings' crèche laughing with his friends, imagining all the adventures he would have as a Padawan, and practicing with his lightsaber in the sparring room until Master [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle") ordered him to bed.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

When the future Jedi Master [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova") first joined the Jedi Order, he became close friends with Jinn, who helped Cordova learn about and get used to Coruscant.[[15]](#cite_note-JediSurvivor-15)

### Apprentice to Dooku[]

#### Becoming a Jedi[]

Around [68 BBY](/wiki/68_BBY "68 BBY"),[[16]](#cite_note-68_BBY-16) when he presented himself to his new Master in Dooku's quarters, Dooku observed that Jinn was frightened. After a moment of silence, and with pressing from Dooku, Jinn confessed that he was. When asked why, after looking into himself through the fear, Jinn answered that he was not afraid of Dooku, but of not becoming a Jedi, that he was afraid of failing and of not being worthy. Dooku then summarized it as Jinn being afraid of himself, of a future not being the one he wanted. Jinn confirmed it, fearing that Dooku would reject him for his cowardice. Dooku instead said that it was very wise, surprising Jinn. Smiling, Dooku explained that most Padawans would deny their fear, and even if they admitted it, they would not have Jinn's self-knowledge. Dooku further praised Jinn for his honesty, insight, and intelligence.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

To help Jinn understand the Jedi Temple more completely, Dooku then took him throughout most of the Temple, including the Padawans' sparring dojo, a dojo where [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") trained, and the [Great Assembly Room](/wiki/Great_Assembly_Room "Great Assembly Room"). Jinn also saw the various meditation chambers, which he didn't find as exciting, but still interesting. On the other hand, Jinn spent long minutes in the arboretum, wandering through the trees, ferns, and flowers of a thousand different worlds. Their last stop was the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives"), where they examined [holocrons](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") of various eras, not to study them, but simply for Jinn to learn his way around. While doing so, an ancient holocron, more ancient and of a different shape than the rest, caught Jinn's eye. When he questioned his Master about it, he was shocked by the expression on Dooku's face, almost as if he considered it an enemy. Dooku answered that it was a holocron of Jedi prophecies. Jinn asked if there are Jedi prophets, to which Dooku replied not any longer. He explained to Jinn that the mystics sought undue knowledge of the future, which led them down dangerous paths. The dark side often tempted those drawn too deeply into them. Dooku then finished by saying that is why the Jedi study prophecy no longer, then turned to leave, which meant Jinn had to follow. Jinn then asked Dooku if just wanting to know the future can lead to the dark side. Dooku replied that it takes more than that. This was Qui-Gon's first encounter with the holocron of prophecies, and it would not be the last.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

 [![Jinn first raised his lightsaber in battle on Shurrupak.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/QuiGonJinn-Strata.png/revision/latest?cb=20251123193233) [![Jinn first raised his lightsaber in battle on Shurrupak.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/QuiGonJinn-Strata.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20251123193233)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/QuiGonJinn-Strata.png/revision/latest?cb=20251123193233) 

Jinn first raised his lightsaber in battle on Shurrupak.

 

After four months as a Padawan, the Council sent him with his master to [Shurrupak](/wiki/Shurrupak "Shurrupak") to participate in a battle on its surface, which was Qui-Gon's very first. While the shuttle they were in approached the planet under heavy fire, a nervous Jinn reassured himself that he was ready for battle, looking to his Master Dooku as an example to aspire to as a fearless Jedi. As they arrived at [Primus Base](/wiki/Primus_Base "Primus Base"), Qui-Gon had his first meeting with [Rael Averross](/wiki/Rael_Averross "Rael Averross"), Dooku's first Padawan and a famous lightsaber duelist. After greeting each other heartily, Dooku introduced Rael to his new Padawan. While Dooku then conferred with the generals, Rael put one hand on the still-nervous Jinn's shoulder. Rather than comforting Jinn about the battle, Rael instead commented that Dooku is hard to get to know and offered to help Qui-Gon out. Since he was Dooku's previous Padawan, Rael told Qui-Gon that he could ask him any questions that he might not feel comfortable asking Dooku yet and be his sparring partner if he wanted. With his first battle looming ahead, Qui-Gon accepted his offer. As they, too, went to talk to the generals, Qui-Gon felt as though Rael Averross was the link between the Padawan he was and the Jedi Knight he desperately wished to be. He viewed his journey to be easier now that he had a friend to show him the path.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

Sometime after that battle, Qui-Gon was doing homework in Dooku's quarters while his Master was in conference with an official from [Badtibira](/wiki/Badtibira "Badtibira"). He then had a surprise visit from Rael Averross, who greeted Jinn warmly. Qui-Gon greeted him with a similar warmth, then asked what he was doing there. Rael explained that he had just returned from Shurrupak, then asked what Jinn was doing in Dooku's quarters since he wouldn't be returning for another few hours. Jinn explained that Dooku lets him do his homework in his quarters if he doesn't disturb him. In this case, Jinn was reporting on the different schools of theosophy a century ago. Upon Rael's grimace and questioning, if he had angered Dooku somehow, Jinn admitted that he chose the topic despite knowing that it wouldn't be interesting because he thought it would be easy. It wasn't.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

Upon receiving a negative from Jinn if it was too late to change his topic, Rael grinned, and motioning for Qui-Gon to follow him, offered to show him some history worth studying. They went to the Jedi Archives, and together they studied the one and only holocron that had ever interested Jinn: the one that held the ancient prophecies. They were all fascinating to him, and Qui-Gon kept reading, unable to stop. He asked Rael if the ancient mystics had these visions in trances, to which he confirmed. After contemplating these prophecies, Jinn remarked that Dooku said he should ignore this holocron and that he doesn't believe in the prophecies. This confused Rael since Dooku, he said, was the one who introduced Rael to it and that it used to be that one could hardly pry the holocron out of his quarters. Qui-Gon said that he didn't know when or why that changed and that Dooku didn't explain. A surprised Rael said he would ask Dooku about it and remarked that Dooku had changed a lot. Qui-Gon protested, surprising Rael, then said not until he's finished his report. Rael then laughed so loud he received a stern look from [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu").[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

#### Tracking Shenda Mol and love life on Felucia[]

:   "*I have a little game I play. I need more kills to win—though, of course, I'm only competing with myself. That's the only competition that really matters, you know. More people ought to un­derstand that.*"
:   ―Shenda Mol, to Qui-Gon Jinn[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

Jinn and his Jedi Master Dooku became part of a [Numidian Prime](/wiki/Numidian_Prime "Numidian Prime") [strike team](/wiki/Numidian_Prime_strike_team "Numidian Prime strike team"). They were assembled to track and find the notorious [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen "Falleen") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Shenda Mol](/wiki/Shenda_Mol "Shenda Mol"). They eventually tracked her at her [hideout](/wiki/Mol%27s_hideout "Mol's hideout") on the planet Numidian Prime. While searching for her hideout, Mol captured Jinn. Before Mol could kill Jinn, Dooku struck her down with [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") to save his apprentice, causing Jinn a degree of concern.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

Jinn later confided what Dooku did to Rael Averross, though at the time, Averross expressed that he was not all too concerned regarding his former master's conduct.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) In [60 BBY](/wiki/60_BBY "60 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) Jinn went through trials on the Outer Rim planet [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia")[[18]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_new-18) when he fell in love with [someone](/wiki/Unidentified_individual_(Qui-Gon_Jinn) "Unidentified individual (Qui-Gon Jinn)"),[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) beginning a romantic[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) and physical relationship. As the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") forbade romantic relationships,[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) Jinn found his commitment to the Jedi ways tested, but he ultimately stayed loyal to the Jedi Order.[[18]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_new-18) He would, however, keep a [Mustafar fire diamond](/wiki/Mustafar_fire_diamond "Mustafar fire diamond") that was given to him on Felucia as a memento.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

At some point during his apprenticeship, Jinn met the [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") [Brennonn](/wiki/Brennonn "Brennonn") and befriended her. They shared many adventures together, with Brennonn saving Jinn on two occasions. During the second of those adventures, events transpired that resulted in Jinn feeling as though they saved each other. He also came to know the Wookiee [Balfus](/wiki/Balfus "Balfus").[[19]](#cite_note-Life_Day-19)

#### Rescuing Senator Dagonet's son[]

:   "*Your actions saved many lives today.*"  
    "*Just thinking in the moment, Master.*"  
    "*Well, then. You're a much wiser man than I, Qui-Gon Jinn.*"  
    "*Thanks to your teachings.*"
:   ―Dooku and Qui-Gon Jinn on his actions during the rescue mission[[9]](#cite_note-Justice-9)

 [![Qui-Gon Jinn and Dooku were sent on a mission to locate Senator Dagonet's son.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Justice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194214) [![Qui-Gon Jinn and Dooku were sent on a mission to locate Senator Dagonet's son.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Justice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20221026194214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Justice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221026194214) 

Qui-Gon Jinn and Dooku were sent on a mission to locate Senator Dagonet's son.

 

During his time as Dooku's Padawan, Jinn and Dooku had been sent on a mission to rescue the [son](/wiki/Uriel_Dagonet "Uriel Dagonet") of Republic [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Dagonet](/wiki/Dagonet "Dagonet"), who was being held captive by the residents of the Senator's home planet. After their investigation, they discovered that the Dagonet was allowing his people to starve for his own personal greed and corruption. The kidnappers abducted Dagonet's son to protest his inhumane policies and discovered that Dagonet's son was yet unharmed. Dagonet arrived to rescue his son, resulting in a brief shootout between the Senator's forces and the Jedi-backed kidnappers. During a lull in the firefight, Dagonet threatened to burn the entire village down and many others to make an example of them. An enraged Dooku began Force-choking Dagonet with the intent to kill him, but Qui-Gon released Dagonet's son and managed to defuse the situation without any further violence. In the aftermath, Dooku commended Qui-Gon's actions and praised him as a wiser man than him.[[9]](#cite_note-Justice-9)

#### Investigating at the Dragonfire Air Rally[]

At one point, both he and Dooku were invited by council member [Jor Aerith](/wiki/Jor_Aerith "Jor Aerith") to join her in representing the Jedi at the annual Coruscant [Dragonfire Air Rally](/wiki/Dragonfire_Air_Rally "Dragonfire Air Rally") in hopes of making a good impression on the [Candovant](/wiki/Candovant "Candovant") ambassador who had invited her. Dooku agreed to attend and took the opportunity to teach Qui-Gon some Candovant customs, but while they were there, they ran into [Ramil](/wiki/Ramil "Ramil"), whom Qui-Gon learned was Dooku's brother, much to his shock. Qui-Gon and Dooku learned that Ramill was was participating in the [race](/wiki/Forty-eighth_annual_Dragonfire_Air_Rally "Forty-eighth annual Dragonfire Air Rally"). While Ramil did very well in the race, it quickly became apparent his [Airspeeder](/wiki/Airspeeder "Airspeeder") was sabotaged and it crashed. Qui-Gon and Dooku discreetly went to see what had happened, and while there they discovered the Investigator was trying to cover up the incident. Following the man, they found he was working for a [Jenet](/wiki/Jenet "Jenet") crime boss named [Cenevax](/wiki/Cenevax "Cenevax"). Ignoring a message from Aerith asking them to return to the races, they chose to confront and captured the criminal, and while questioning her they realized that she was privy to Council communications, as Cenevax made clear she knew they that had been recalled and were disobeying order by being there. With this information, Dooku deduced that she had a spy on the Council, much to the shock of Qui-Gon.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Dooku and Qui-Gon escorted Cenevax to the Council Chamber, where Dooku made his accusation, and discovered that Jedi Master [Braylon](/wiki/Yula_Braylon "Yula Braylon") was the spy. Further investigation revealed that Cenevax had been blackmailing her with the fact that Arath Tarrex, the latter being Dooku's old classmate and was also shockingly revealed to be in fact her son. Qui-Gon and Dooku confronted and exposed Tarrex, who was then taken into custody for his actions and also for having sold out his mother's influence to criminals. As the Temple guards were escorting Tarrex, Dooku encouraged Qui-Gon to go with them and ensure that the guards treated him well, both of which Qui-Gon agreed to do. Following this event being resolved, Braylon was removed from her seat on the council because of her actions, Dooku joined the Council.[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10)

Jinn became a Jedi Knight around [58 BBY](/wiki/58_BBY "58 BBY").[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17)

### Master to Obi-Wan Kenobi[]

#### Becoming a mentor[]

 [![Becoming the mentor to Obi-Wan Kenobi, Qui-Gon Jinn sought to teach him the best he could.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/BeMindful-AORObiWan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20241026231334) [![Becoming the mentor to Obi-Wan Kenobi, Qui-Gon Jinn sought to teach him the best he could.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/BeMindful-AORObiWan1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/265?cb=20241026231334)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/BeMindful-AORObiWan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20241026231334) 

Becoming the mentor to Obi-Wan Kenobi, Qui-Gon Jinn sought to teach him the best he could.

 

Jinn became a [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") Master in his own right, a master who developed an independent attitude towards the Jedi Order. Others saw him as a maverick Jedi, one who would disobey the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") if he felt it was the right decision.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) In [44 BBY](/wiki/44_BBY "44 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) Jinn took on a Padawan named [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), who believed that Jinn could've been a member of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") if he followed the Code,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) though as Kenobi knew, Jinn had rejected an offer to join.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) On one occasion, Kenobi watched in silence as his master told the council he disagreed with them. At another point, the master and apprentice sparred, with Jinn complimenting Kenobi's skill. On another occasion, the two visited a plain and overlooked its native creatures, giving Jinn the chance to teach Kenobi about how the Force existed in all the life that surrounded them.[[20]](#cite_note-AoR_Obi-Wan-20)

Jinn was able to sense whenever Kenobi was discontent, which proved useful on some missions, yet also annoyed Kenobi.[[21]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-21) At one point, Jinn and Kenobi traveled to the planet [Lah'mu](/wiki/Lah%27mu "Lah'mu") to visit a [fortress](/wiki/Chief%27s_fortress "Chief's fortress").[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11) Jinn also maintained contact with his old Master after taking on Kenobi and spoke highly of his Padawan to Dooku.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_II-12) While Dooku left the Jedi Order after the [invasion of Serenno](/wiki/Incident_on_Serenno "Incident on Serenno")[[10]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-10) in [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) secretly becoming a [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") to the elusive [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") sometime later,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_II-12) he was still allowed to visit the Jedi Temple.[[22]](#cite_note-Padawan_Novel-22) Dooku's decision to leave the Jedi came as a shock to Jinn, who felt lost for a time as he grappled with feelings of doubt and fear. However, Jinn trusted in the Jedi teachings and himself, which allowed him to recover and replace his shaken feelings with resolve.[[23]](#cite_note-Resolve-23) At some point, Jinn met the [Togorian](/wiki/Togorian "Togorian") Jedi [Jak'zin](/wiki/Jak%27zin "Jak'zin"), who had also looked up to Dooku.[[24]](#cite_note-AoR_Dooku-24)

Jinn taught Kenobi as best he could, although Kenobi did not always agree with his master's teaching strategies. Despite his Padawan's clear proficiencies in lightsaber techniques, Jinn held Kenobi to practicing only basic methods, which impacted his apprentice's confidence and their relationship. Although Jinn did so to not rush his apprentice and allow Kenobi to carve out his own distinct style out of mastery of the fundamental [cadences](/wiki/Cadence "Cadence"), his lack of clarity on his teaching philosophy hurt Kenobi.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

At some point, Obi-Wan came up with the idea of a new weapon powered by kyber crystals which consisted of two short-bladed sabers each attached to a thin chain. After hearing this idea from Kenobi, Qui-Gon told his padawan that lightsabers were about how the Jedi wished to be seen, and that was not intended to be a display of power. That lesson resonated with his young Padawan, who would carry it for years to come.[[25]](#cite_note-The_Lesson_OW-25)

#### Protecting Duchess Satine[]

:   "*Master Qui-Gon and I spent a year on Mandalore, protecting the duchess from insurgents who had threatened her world. They sent bounty hunters after us. We were always on the run, living hand to mouth, never sure what the next day would bring.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[26]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-26)

 [![Satine Kryze, whom Kenobi and Jinn were assigned to protect](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/SatineKryze-Corruption.png/revision/latest?cb=20130509231427) [![Satine Kryze, whom Kenobi and Jinn were assigned to protect](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/SatineKryze-Corruption.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20130509231427)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/SatineKryze-Corruption.png/revision/latest?cb=20130509231427) 

Satine Kryze, whom Kenobi and Jinn were assigned to protect

 

Between circa [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY") and circa [39 BBY](/wiki/39_BBY "39 BBY"),[[27]](#cite_note-41-39_Date_Note-27) a [civil war](/wiki/Great_Clan_Wars "Great Clan Wars") began to rage on the planet [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"), with the world's [martial traditionalists](/wiki/Martial_traditionalists "Martial traditionalists") fighting against a reformist faction known as the [New Mandalorians](/wiki/New_Mandalorians "New Mandalorians"). The leader of the New Mandalorian movement, [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"),[[28]](#cite_note-Fact_File-28) became a target for the traditionalists, who hired [bounty hunters](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") to eliminate her. However, Jinn and Kenobi were sent on an extended mission to Mandalore, where they were assigned to protect Kryze.[[26]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-26)

Jinn and Kenobi spent a [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") on Mandalore with Kryze, remaining on the run from the bounty hunters. The three remained unsure of what the future would bring, but they continued their effort to survive, living hand to mouth everyday. During the mission, Kenobi developed romantic feelings for Kryze.[[26]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-26) Jinn became aware of the unlikely romance between his apprentice and the noble.[[21]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-21) Eventually, the civil war came to an end, with the New Mandalorians coming to power and Kryze becoming the ruler of Mandalore. Although Kenobi would have left the Jedi and stayed behind to be with her had she asked him to, Kryze never did, so he and Jinn left the planet.[[26]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-26)

#### Life Day adventure[]

 [![Jinn and Kenobi face off against Korgan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Rescue_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn.png/revision/latest?cb=20210625130331) [![Jinn and Kenobi face off against Korgan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Rescue_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20210625130331)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Rescue_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn.png/revision/latest?cb=20210625130331) 

Jinn and Kenobi face off against Korgan.

 

Around [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) Jinn told Kenobi he would be taking him on a training exercise, keeping it secret that they would be going to observe the Wookiees' celebration of [Life Day](/wiki/Life_Day "Life Day") on[[19]](#cite_note-Life_Day-19) the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet")[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate-1) [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk") in the village of his old friend Brennonn, who had accepted his offer to visit. After entering the village, Jinn advised his Padawan to remain patient after the young man expressed confusion, reminding him to focus on what was instead of what he had expected. Though Kenobi found it hard to focus amid a celebration, Jinn continued their visit, educating his Padawan about Wookiee culture before asking what he made of it. Pleased with Kenobi's answer that it was as if the Wookiees were celebrating the Force, he explained the unconventional training he wanted Kenobi to partake in; he was asking him to focus on the energy of Kashyyyk, given that it was the Force. He then informed his Padawan they would speak with the Wookiees when Kenobi revealed he felt something different.[[19]](#cite_note-Life_Day-19)

Suddenly, the two Jedi were interrupted when Brennonn spotted Jinn, resulting in the Wookiee hugging him from how such she had missed him. Jinn shared her sentiment and began to introduce her to Kenobi, only for her to hug him as well. After Jinn explained his history with the Wookiee to Kenobi and thanked her for letting them come, she told him that Balfus was missing. As Jinn inquired about what actions she had taken concerning the missing Wookiee, both he and Kenobi felt a [disturbance in the Force](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force"); several [Trandoshan](/wiki/Trandoshan "Trandoshan") hunters suddenly attacked the village, launching nets from the trees to kidnap more Wookiees. Jinn and Kenobi fought against the Trandoshans, defeating many of them. However, Jinn himself was eventually captured when he demanded the hunters to surrender. Along with the captured Wookiees, Jinn was taken away by a [MSP80 Pteropter hover pod](/wiki/MSP80_Pteropter_hover_pod "MSP80 Pteropter hover pod").[[19]](#cite_note-Life_Day-19)

Although Jinn, as he was taken away, had told Kenobi it was up to him to rescue the Wookiees,[[19]](#cite_note-Life_Day-19) the Jedi Master tried to negotiate the Wookiees' release with the Trandoshans' leader, [Korgan](/wiki/Korgan "Korgan"). However, Korgan wanted to capture Kenobi too, and Jinn warned him that his greed would have been his downfall. Jinn waited in his cage until Kenobi [arrived](/wiki/Rescue_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn "Rescue of Qui-Gon Jinn"). Kenobi pretended to surrender but, when Korgan was distracted, he opened Jinn's cage with the Force. Jinn [Force-pulled](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") his lightsaber and ignited it. As Jinn was freed, many Wookiees arrived to support the two Jedi: the Trandoshans, being outnumbered, surrendered and freed the Wookiee prisoners. After returning to the village, the Life Day celebration began.[[29]](#cite_note-Life_Day_2-29)

#### Mission to Pijal[]

:   "*I've never been to Pijal.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

 [![The mission to Pijal](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/PijalCover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210404112612) [![The mission to Pijal](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/PijalCover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210404112612)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/PijalCover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210404112612) 

The mission to Pijal

 

In [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) Jinn and Kenobi undertook a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Teth "Mission to Teth") to [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth") to thwart [Wanbo](/wiki/Wanbo "Wanbo") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt"). The two Jedi escaped Teth, but not without complications including a key miscommunication between master and apprentice. Upon returning to Coruscant, the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") extended to Jinn an invitation to join their ranks, as with Master [Poli Dapatian](/wiki/Poli_Dapatian "Poli Dapatian") was stepping down by that month's end. Jinn was shocked to be asked due to his disagreements with the Council on various occasions, and while he was initially pleased to hear the offer, he thought of his Padawan, who he would have to pass on to a new master if he were to accept. While it would solve the growing problems between them, Jinn felt guilt at the thought of it and thus told the Council that he would meditate on their proposition.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

Meanwhile, a [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") dispute erupted on the [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") planet [Pijal](/wiki/Pijal "Pijal"). A performance troupe known as the [Opposition](/wiki/Opposition "Opposition") that began playing political pranks to protest a [treaty](/wiki/Governance_Treaty "Governance Treaty") signing that would end the absolute monarchy on Pijal, allow the world to join the Republic, and give more power to [Czerka Corporation](/wiki/Czerka_Arms "Czerka Arms") was thought to be making increasingly violent attacks nearing the treaty's signing. Jinn's old friend Rael Averross requested Jinn and his Padawan's assistance to end the dispute and ensure the signing of the treaty. The Council [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Pijal "Mission to Pijal") Jinn and his Padawan to Pijal to help. However, as the mission began, Kenobi became aware of the offer presented to Jinn regarding the Jedi Council when the two met with [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Kirames Kaj](/wiki/Kirames_Kaj "Kirames Kaj"). Jinn felt great shame at not being the first to tell his Padawan learner. Before they left, Jinn sought out Kenobi and the Padawan's dojo. He attempted to apologize for not being the first to tell him the news and said that he had several reservations that he had to dwell on before committing to the position, but Kenobi made a sarcastic reply. Jinn told his Padawan that he would continue to discuss the matter when Kenobi was in a more rational mood, and when Kenobi quipped again, Jinn sadly said that he supposed that the Force always allowed things to turn out for the best. As they traveled to Pijal, the tension between them grew.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

Jinn and Kenobi both were briefed on the situation, learning that Averross served Crown [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Fanry](/wiki/Fanry "Fanry"), who was only fourteen years old, as an advisor and that he needed to protect her from the Opposition as she waited to take Pijal's throne. Jinn and Averross became reacquainted quickly, although Jinn was skeptical of several of Averross's choices during his service, as Averross also loosely interpreted the Jedi Code. As he and Kenobi began to do more investigating on [Pijal's moon](/wiki/Pijal%27s_moon "Pijal's moon"), they encountered two jewel thieves, [Pax Maripher](/wiki/Pax_Maripher "Pax Maripher") and [Rahara Wick](/wiki/Rahara_Wick "Rahara Wick"). Although Maripher was very abrasive towards Jinn, Wick was more cooperative. Onboard their ship, the [*Meryx*](/wiki/Meryx_(starship) "Meryx (starship)"), Jinn recruited the two to help them find the terrorists that posed a threat to the treaty. Shortly after returning, Jinn received a vision of the event, which turned into a bloody battle. He brought it to Averross's attention, but the older Jedi did not share his level of concern.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

As their investigation continued, Jinn eventually met with the Opposition's leader, [Halin Azucca](/wiki/Halin_Azucca "Halin Azucca"), and learned that her group was being framed. Although they had peacefully made demonstrations against the treaty, the violent terrorist acts that had alerted the Republic were not caused by Azucca's people. As Qui-Gon learned of the complications surrounding the treaty due to the lack of Pijali representation and the heavy influence gained by the [Czerka Corporation](/wiki/Czerka_Arms "Czerka Arms"), he decided to oppose the treaty himself and refused to act as a Republic representative.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

However, eventually, the Jedi discovered that Fanry was deceiving them and had been building a military group called the blackguards, framing the Opposition to restore the full monarchy. At the coronation, she rejected the treaty as well as the Republic's influence, proving herself to having been underestimated by the Jedi. Ready to remove Czerka influence from the system by force, she prepared to attack their ships. Jinn attempted to convince her to stop and prevent the innocent casualties that were the Czerka slaves onboard the ships, but when she refused, Jinn took matters into his own hands, and with the help of Kenobi as well as their two new friends Maripher and Wick, they succeeded in saving the slaves. After the mission, Jinn decided to stick with training Kenobi and declined the offer to join the Jedi Council.[[11]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-11)

#### Helping Master Yoda[]

 [![Qui Gon Jinn and Yoda discuss a disturbance in the force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/YodaAndQuiGonTalk-2015StarWars26.png/revision/latest?cb=20181208193133) [![Qui Gon Jinn and Yoda discuss a disturbance in the force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/YodaAndQuiGonTalk-2015StarWars26.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20181208193133)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/YodaAndQuiGonTalk-2015StarWars26.png/revision/latest?cb=20181208193133) 

Qui Gon Jinn and Yoda discuss a disturbance in the force.

 

Around 40 BBY,[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) Jinn and Kenobi were operating near a [planet](/wiki/Botor "Botor") that served as a base of the [Flesh Mongers](/wiki/Flesh_Mongers "Flesh Mongers") pirate group, flying a [pair](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn%27s_Aethersprite "Qui-Gon Jinn's Aethersprite") [of](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_Delta-7_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Obi-Wan Kenobi's Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor") [Delta-7 *Aethersprite*-class light interceptors](/wiki/Delta-7_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor"). The two received a message from the planet's surface from Jedi Master [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), who asked for assistance. Landing on the planet, Jinn and Kenobi discovered that Yoda had taken out the entire pirate gang to rescue a young Force-sensitive [child](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling"), known as [Lo](/wiki/Lo "Lo"), as the pirate had planned to sell him due to his Force abilities.[[30]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-30)

Yoda asked Jinn and Kenobi to escort the infant to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace"), with Yoda assuring Lo that he was in safe hands with Jinn. Jinn expressed that he was happy to help out as they had been so close. While the two conversed, Kenobi took particular interest in that Yoda took out an entire room of pirates and was totally in awe. Jinn then proceeded to ask Yoda if everything was all right, to which the revered master replied that he could sense a calling [disturbance in the Force](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force") that he felt he must follow. Jinn noted that he could not feel the presence himself, but offered to join him on his quest if he so wanted. As Yoda climbed into his [starship](/wiki/Yoda%27s_Delta-7_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Yoda's Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor"), he responded that he felt it was simply a calling for him alone and embarked on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Vagadarr_Prime "Mission to Vagadarr Prime") to a [planet](/wiki/Vagadarr_Prime "Vagadarr Prime") in the [Vagadarr system](/wiki/Vagadarr_system "Vagadarr system"), where he became involved in a [tribal war](/wiki/War_on_Vagadarr_Prime "War on Vagadarr Prime") between the planet's native inhabitants.[[30]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-30)

### Truths of the Force[]

#### Discovering the secrets of life after death[]

Sometime during his life, Jinn began discovering the secrets to [manifesting his consciousness](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") after [death](/wiki/Death "Death").[[31]](#cite_note-Voices-31) He traveled to a [planet](/wiki/Wellspring_of_Life "Wellspring of Life") strong with the Force, a [world](/wiki/Planet "Planet") that legend said was the birthplace of life and the origin of [midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian"). He learned from five [Force Priestesses](/wiki/Force_Priestesses "Force Priestesses") who had retained their consciousness after death.[[32]](#cite_note-Force-Planet-SWE-32) He learned that, when a living thing died, its life passed through the [Living Force](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force") and into the [Cosmic Force](/wiki/Cosmic_Force "Cosmic Force") to become one with the Force.[[31]](#cite_note-Voices-31)

As the Living Force and Cosmic Force existed in tandem, it became possible for one to retain consciousness and physically manifest themselves after death. Jinn was considered worthy of the knowledge of eternal life and secretly began his training to unlock its mysteries fully.[[31]](#cite_note-Voices-31) He also learned from a [Shaman of the Whills](/wiki/Shaman_of_the_Whills "Shaman of the Whills") that achieving eternal consciousness required absolute selflessness.[[5]](#cite_note-SWEQui-GonJinn-5)

#### Questioning his purpose[]

:   "*Being called a coward isn't what bothered me, Master Yoda. It was being called a great warrior.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33)

 [![Qui-Gon during the rescue of Th'er](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/ConflictOnBrin-AORQuiGonJinn1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181214064154) [![Qui-Gon during the rescue of Th'er](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/ConflictOnBrin-AORQuiGonJinn1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181214064154)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/ConflictOnBrin-AORQuiGonJinn1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181214064154) 

Qui-Gon during the rescue of Th'er

 

Jinn began experiencing an inner turmoil over how the Jedi should interact with the Force. Although Yoda sensed that internal debate in the man, Jinn continued on with his Jedi duties for sometime.[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33) In [37 BBY](/wiki/37_BBY "37 BBY"),[[34]](#cite_note-Date_37BBY-34) when Jinn and Kenobi were sent to the planet [Bri'n](/wiki/Bri%27n "Bri'n") to establish negotiations between the the [Priestess](/wiki/Priestess "Priestess") [Th'er](/wiki/Th%27er "Th'er") of Wood and the [Metal Clan](/wiki/Metal_Clan "Metal Clan"), Kenobi stayed within their [*Eta*-class shuttle](/wiki/Eta-class_shuttle "Eta-class shuttle") while Jinn met with the Priestess's rivals. When the Metal Clan instead tried to kill Jinn and the Priestess as a justification to begin cutting down the world's trees, he moved to defend Th'er and escape with her. Deflecting many [blaster bolts](/wiki/Laser "Laser") with his lightsaber, the Jedi contacted Kenobi to start their [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle") and inform him about the failed negotiations. After being surrounded by the Metal Clan, Th'er proclaimed that Jinn was a warrior who could take down all who opposed her, yet Jinn instead used [Force jump](/wiki/Force_jump "Force jump") to escape with her aboard their shuttle, ordering Kenobi to take them to Coruscant so as to protect the Priestess.[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33)

Th'er was nevertheless disgusted by Coruscant—viewing it as a city of metal—and demanded Jinn to act as a warrior, ordering him to cut down every member of the Metal Clan. Although Jinn informed her that was not the path of the Jedi Order, Th'er felt Jinn was instead a coward who did not live up to the legends that proclaimed the Jedi to be great soldiers. Greatly distressed at being called a warrior, he returned to the Jedi Temple, where he did not report to the Jedi High Council. Deciding to confront Jinn over his internal turmoil, Yoda located the Jedi Master on one of the Temple's balconies under the pretense of asking for him to report to the Council. Aware that Kenobi had filed his own report, Jinn quickly saw through Yoda's claim, leading to a discussion about how the Jedi should act between the two masters.[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33)

Even though Yoda and him had different opinions, they both agreed that Jinn should seek answers. Needing a world full of life to find a deep communion with the Force, Jinn—travelling off Coruscant in his [Delta-7 Jedi Interceptor](/wiki/Delta-7_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor") with his [astromech droid](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn%27s_astromech_droid "Qui-Gon Jinn's astromech droid")—trusted the Force to guide him to answers, resulting in him coming out of hyperspace above a [charted but unnamed world](/wiki/Unidentified_world_(Qui-Gon_Jinn) "Unidentified world (Qui-Gon Jinn)"). After leaving his ship and admiring the planet's beauty, Jinn quickly felt the presence of the dark side on the world and noticed how a spreading darkness was starting to corrupt the planet. Unsure whether the Force wanted him to stop it or learn from it, Jinn continued until he found a temple and sat its throne. Pondering whether he would find light in the dark monument, Jinn entered a frightening [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision").[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33)

 [![In a Force vision, Qui-Gon Jinn learned that unchecked violence would only lead to the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/JinnConsumedByDarkness-AORQuiGonJinn1.png/revision/latest?cb=20210806202006) [![In a Force vision, Qui-Gon Jinn learned that unchecked violence would only lead to the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/JinnConsumedByDarkness-AORQuiGonJinn1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210806202006)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/JinnConsumedByDarkness-AORQuiGonJinn1.png/revision/latest?cb=20210806202006) 

In a Force vision, Qui-Gon Jinn learned that unchecked violence would only lead to the dark side.

 

In his vision, Jinn—his skin and [Jedi robes](/wiki/Jedi_apparel "Jedi apparel") covered in marks—was surrounded by red humanoid beings who grew out of dark tendrils. Although at least one of these beings tried to attack him as he fought, Jinn quickly ignited his lightsaber and cut the beings down, only for the red coloration to vanish from those he had killed. Jinn saw he had murdered Jedi, and the same darkness that he had seen on their bodies began to consume him; by choosing violence, the dark side had gained power over him. As the darkness wrapped across his face, Jinn awoke from his vision horrified, only to see the light side had entered into the monument. He realized the Force had taught him he could find balance that could be achieved without conflict, as unchecked violence would make the Jedi turn into what they sought to confront. In fact, he found that some of the planet's dark corruption had instead formed into flowers, existing in harmony with the light.[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33)

Leaving the planet—albeit with new questions about the nature of the Force—and returning to Coruscant, Jinn found Th'er in one of the city world's parks, where offered to help her find off-world allies with whom to fight against the Metal Clan. Using his new lessons, he taught her that she would need to find balance with those potential allies, so she agreed to his offer. During the night, he again met with Yoda on a temple balcony, leading to another discussion about the Force. Speaking with the Grand Master, Jinn defended finding balance in the Force, believing the Jedi could not be too rigid yet could also not give into the dark side.[[33]](#cite_note-AoR-Q-GJ1-33)

#### Jedi operations[]

 [![Qui-Gon Jinn, alongside Plo Koon and Depa Billaba on Oosalon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/JediOnOosalon-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190418005506) [![Qui-Gon Jinn, alongside Plo Koon and Depa Billaba on Oosalon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/JediOnOosalon-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190418005506)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/JediOnOosalon-TheWeapon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190418005506) 

Qui-Gon Jinn, alongside Plo Koon and Depa Billaba on Oosalon.

 

In [34 BBY](/wiki/34_BBY "34 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Timelines-17) Jinn—alongside Jedi Masters [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon"), and [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba")—was sent to the planet [Oosalon](/wiki/Oosalon "Oosalon") by Supreme Chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") due to the actions of the [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") [Guattako](/wiki/Guattako "Guattako"), who was backed by the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan") and had kidnapped children to serve as soldiers. Being a planet that had around 80,000 [kilometers](/wiki/Kilometer "Kilometer") worth of tunnels, the Jedi would be unable to find the base of [Guattako's army](/wiki/Guattako%27s_army "Guattako's army"), so they made a plan that Windu would be purposely captured, allowing him to send a signal in the Force to lead his fellow Jedi to Guattako. Although Jinn and his fellow Jedi—joined by at least two soldiers—were unable to make it through the tunnels in time to help Windu, the Jedi Master had nevertheless defeated Guattako's army, while the warlord himself had been shot by one of the children he had kidnapped. Thus, Guattako's revolution was thwarted, the children could be return to their homes, and the remaining members of the terrorist army were captured.[[35]](#cite_note-The_Weapon-35)

### War on Naboo[]

#### Failed negotiations[]

:   "*Is it in their nature to make us wait this long?*"  
    "*No. I sense an unusual amount of fear for something as trivial as this trade dispute.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Qui-Gon Jinn — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/TrivialTradeDispute-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192855)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:TrivialTradeDispute-TPM.flac "File:TrivialTradeDispute-TPM.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Ten years prior to the [outbreak](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") [blockaded](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") and planned to [invade](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") it in retaliation for the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic")'s taxation of [trade routes](/wiki/Free_Trade_Zone "Free Trade Zone") in outlying [star](/wiki/Star "Star") systems. Unknown to the Republic, the [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious—secretly Naboo's Senator Palpatine—controlled the Federation and engineered the conflict so he could be elected Supreme Chancellor.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) Before the blockade, Jinn felt that something was amiss and took Kenobi to the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") to read through Senate documents, as they often did whenever Jinn felt something was wrong in the Senate. While reviewing bills concerning the recent tax reforms, Obi-Wan grew listless and Jinn, sensing his apprentice's discomfort, asked him what he thought. Kenobi opined to Jinn that people had too much time on their hands and he did not understand why people spent so much time talking about taxation. Qui-Gon looked up from the file he was reading and admonished Kenobi, telling him that it was a matter of perspective and that the most important thing to the people who submitted the bills was control. Jinn noted that there was a lot of control to lose between the planets and corporations involved in the tax dispute.[[21]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-21)

Obi-Wan questioned why they were personally purviewing the bills, and Jinn replied that they were listening so they could act when they needed to. Obi-Wan teasingly asked if they would act with or without orders, which made Jinn smile, though the Jedi Master informed his apprentice that they were likely to be following orders. Kenobi quipped that, because they would be under the Council's alignment, they would be less likely to be involved in local labor disputes. Bothered by Kenobi's comment, Jinn rebuked that they would also be less likely to kick-start romances with the local nobility. The reference to Duchess Satine let Kenobi know better than to treat such things so trivially, and he changed the subject as they continued reading the taxation bills. Jinn's precautions proved useful as[[21]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-21) Chancellor Finis Valorum dispatched Jinn and Kenobi to Naboo, tasking them with resolving the situation through [diplomatic](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat") means.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

 [![Jinn and Kenobi uncover the Federation invasion force on the command ship.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/Uncovering-the-army.png/revision/latest?cb=20241001023340) [![Jinn and Kenobi uncover the Federation invasion force on the command ship.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/Uncovering-the-army.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20241001023340)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/Uncovering-the-army.png/revision/latest?cb=20241001023340) 

Jinn and Kenobi uncover the Federation invasion force on the command ship.

 

Upon arriving at the Trade Federation [command ship](/wiki/Command_ship "Command ship") *[Saak'ak](/wiki/Saak%27ak "Saak'ak")*, Jinn and Kenobi were escorted into a conference room, where they were told that [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy_of_the_Trade_Federation "Viceroy of the Trade Federation") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray") would greet them. As the Jedi were waiting, the Federation leaders contacted Darth Sidious, informing him that the Chancellor's [ambassadors](/wiki/Ambassador "Ambassador") were [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"). Sidious ordered their execution, while Jinn could sense the fear that the [Neimoidians](/wiki/Neimoidian "Neimoidian") felt, letting Jinn know this wasn't a common trade dispute. These suspicions were confirmed when the Federation flooded the conference room with [poison gas](/wiki/Dioxis "Dioxis") to kill the Jedi. But the two were able to hold their breath long enough for the Federation to open the doors and inadvertently give the Jedi a chance to [escape](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Saak%27ak "Escape from the Saak'ak"). They fought off the [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") waiting outside the door and fled through the corridors, where they made their way into the ventilation system.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Moving through the ventilation shafts, the Jedi made their way to the [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar"), where they saw the Federation Army preparing to mount an invasion of the planet. After Kenobi quipped that Jinn had predicted that the negotiations would be short, the Jedi stowed away aboard [separate ships](/wiki/C-9979_landing_craft "C-9979 landing craft"), which made their way to the planet's surface and planned to warn the Naboo that the invasion was coming.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

#### Rescuing the Queen[]

:   "*The situation here is not what it seems. There is something else behind all this, Your Highness. There is no logic in the Federation's move here. My feelings tell me they will destroy you.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn, to Queen Amidala — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/NoLogic-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192758)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:NoLogic-TPM.flac "File:NoLogic-TPM.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

 [![Jinn and Kenobi meet Jar Jar Binks.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Jar_Jar_meets_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210234240) [![Jinn and Kenobi meet Jar Jar Binks.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Jar_Jar_meets_Jedi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/272?cb=20130210234240)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Jar_Jar_meets_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210234240) 

Jinn and Kenobi meet Jar Jar Binks.

 

Once on the surface, Jinn ventured through a [forest](/wiki/Forest "Forest") to rendezvous with Kenobi and encountered a [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") named [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks"), who latched onto him in the chaos of the Federation invasion. This encounter nearly got them killed as they fell to the ground just in [time](/wiki/Time "Time") to avoid being run over by a Federation [troop carrier](/wiki/Multi-Troop_Transport "Multi-Troop Transport"). Binks swore a [life debt](/wiki/Life_debt "Life debt") to Jinn for saving him, as Jinn tried to get rid of the Gungan. He finally rendezvoused with Kenobi and planned to find shelter, which Binks offered to give them in the [Gungan city](/wiki/Otoh_Gunga "Otoh Gunga") beneath the [ocean](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean"). The Gungan momentarily changed his mind, revealing that he had been [exiled](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") and would be punished for returning; however, Jinn and Kenobi convinced him to take them there to avoid the approaching Federation forces.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Binks led the two Jedi into the Gungan [city](/wiki/City "City"), where how they were immediately apprehended and brought before the [Gungan leaders](/wiki/Gungan_High_Council "Gungan High Council"). Jinn attempted to persuade the Gungan leader, [Boss](/wiki/Boss "Boss") [Nass](/wiki/Rugor_Nass "Rugor Nass"), that the Federation posed a threat to them just as much as they threatened Naboo. But Gungan prejudices against the [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)") were too strong for the Boss to care about what happened on the surface. The Jedi Master used the Force to [telepathically](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") persuade Nass to give them a [bongo](/wiki/Tribubble_bongo "Tribubble bongo") [aquatic](/wiki/Water "Water") [transport](/wiki/Transport "Transport") that the Jedi could use to reach [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed"), the capital of Naboo. Nass was also persuaded to allow Binks to travel with them, as Jinn, claiming the life debt custom, believed the Gungan could be a guide to make it through the planet core and to the capital.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

After traveling through the core and evading multiple large sea creatures, they arrived in Theed and rescued [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), who was taken into Federation custody. Together, along with a number of the queen's [guards](/wiki/Naboo_Palace_Guard "Naboo Palace Guard") and [handmaidens](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Handmaidens "Naboo Royal Handmaidens"), they made their way to a hangar to take the [queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen")'s [starship](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Starship "Naboo Royal Starship") off of Naboo. They were able to board the ship after fighting through many battle [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid") and took the vessel into orbit where they encountered the Federation blockade. They managed to escape, but the ship was damaged and needed to be set down for repairs. Jinn suggested that they land on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"), a [desert](/wiki/Desert "Desert") planet where the [Hutts](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") ruled and the Federation had no presence. Although the queen's lead guard, [Panaka](/wiki/Quarsh_Panaka "Quarsh Panaka"), objected because of the danger posed by the [Hutts](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan"), the decision was made to seek refuge on Tatooine.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

#### Discovery of the Chosen One[]

:   "*Finding him was the will of the Force. I have no doubt of that.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn to the Jedi High Council — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/WillOfTheForce-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192903)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:WillOfTheForce-TPM.flac "File:WillOfTheForce-TPM.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

 [![Jinn chides Binks during a meal with Skywalker and his mother.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Jedi_reflexes.png/revision/latest?cb=20130131153327) [![Jinn chides Binks during a meal with Skywalker and his mother.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Jedi_reflexes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/271?cb=20130131153327)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Jedi_reflexes.png/revision/latest?cb=20130131153327) 

Jinn chides Binks during a meal with Skywalker and his mother.

 

Landing on Tatooine, the crew determined they needed a new [hyperdrive generator](/wiki/T-14_hyperdrive_generator "T-14 hyperdrive generator") to make it to their final destination: Coruscant, the Republic's capital. Jinn decided to venture out into [the local settlement](/wiki/Mos_Espa "Mos Espa") to find a store that would sell a generator. He brought Amidala—masquerading as a royal handmaiden—and Binks along with him. While they were in town,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) everyone on the Royal Starship was left waiting for Jinn's return, leaving them to worry or read to pass the time.[[36]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-36) Jinn, Amidala, and Binks arrived at a [shop](/wiki/Watto%27s_junkshop "Watto's junkshop") owned by a [Toydarian](/wiki/Toydarian "Toydarian") [junk dealer](/wiki/Junk_dealer "Junk dealer"), [Watto](/wiki/Watto "Watto"), who had the parts they needed, but would not accept Republic [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") for payment. Jinn attempted to persuade him that credits would be acceptable telepathically, but the Toydarian was immune to Jedi mind tricks. Jinn left empty-handed, but not before meeting [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), a young boy who was a [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") of Watto's.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Skywalker followed Jinn and the others, where he warned them that a [sandstorm](/wiki/Sandstorm "Sandstorm") was coming and that they would need to find shelter. The boy knew the group would not make it back to their ship in time and brought them back to his [home](/wiki/Skywalker_home "Skywalker home"), where he introduced them to his [mother](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), [Shmi](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars"), who was also one of Watto's slaves. They all shared dinner, where Skywalker deduced that Jinn was a Jedi, having seen his [lightsaber](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn%27s_lightsaber "Qui-Gon Jinn's lightsaber"). Jinn revealed that he and the others were on a critical mission for the Republic and stranded on Tatooine until they could repair their ship. Knowing that it could help them escape, Skywalker volunteered to help by racing in the [Boonta Eve Classic](/wiki/Boonta_Eve_Classic "Boonta Eve Classic") [podrace](/wiki/Podracing "Podracing") and give them the profits to repair their ship if he won. Jinn accepted the offer, though Amidala was unconvinced that trusting their fate to someone they barely knew was the right course.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

The next [day](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day"), Jinn spoke to Watto about entering Skywalker in the race with a [pod](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker%27s_Podracer "Anakin Skywalker's Podracer") that Skywalker had built in secret, and Jinn convinced Watto that it was the Jedi's [pod](/wiki/Podracer "Podracer"). The two agreed that Watto would pay Skywalker's entry fee and collect all of the winnings from a potential victory, except for whatever money Jinn needed to repair his ship. If Skywalker lost, Watto would keep the queen's ship. Watto agreed to the condition, and Skywalker set out to begin getting his pod race-ready.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

In watching Skywalker work on his pod, Jinn told Shmi he could sense a Jedi's potential in the boy. Jinn wondered who Skywalker's father was and was intrigued to hear Shmi had conceived her son without a father. Later that night, Jinn tested the boy's midi-chlorian count and sent the sample to Kenobi on the queen's ship, who told his master that Skywalker's midi-chlorian count was over 20,000—higher than any known Jedi. Through the supposed virgin [birth](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") and the midi-chlorian count, Jinn came to believe that Skywalker was the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") of Jedi prophecy, a being who would bring balance to the Force and stop the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

With the belief that Skywalker was the Chosen One, Jinn knew that he should bring Skywalker to the [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") on Coruscant to be trained as a Jedi. Jinn approached Watto with a new wager: if the boy were to win, Watto would free Skywalker and his mother. Watto scoffed at the idea of freeing two slaves, but he did agree to release one if Skywalker won. However, he left it up to chance and threw a small multi-[colored](/wiki/Color "Color") [cube](/wiki/Chance_cube "Chance cube"); if it landed on blue, Skywalker would be the slave in question. Jinn [used](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") the Force to help it land on blue, and Watto agreed to free Skywalker if he won the race—but, according to Watto, the [Dug](/wiki/Dug "Dug") [racer](/wiki/Podracer_(profession) "Podracer (profession)") [Sebulba](/wiki/Sebulba "Sebulba") was sure to win.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

 [![Jinn fights Darth Maul on Tatooine, the first known encounter between Jedi and Sith for a thousand years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/JinnVsMaul-SWBC67.png/revision/latest?cb=20240220052314) [![Jinn fights Darth Maul on Tatooine, the first known encounter between Jedi and Sith for a thousand years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/JinnVsMaul-SWBC67.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240220052314)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/JinnVsMaul-SWBC67.png/revision/latest?cb=20240220052314) 

Jinn fights Darth Maul on Tatooine, the first known encounter between Jedi and Sith for a thousand years.

 

The race began later that day, and Skywalker emerged victoriously. Watto, who lost everything betting on Sebulba, freed the boy as per their agreement. Jinn took what profits he needed to repair the ship, gave the rest to Skywalker and his mother, and told them that Skywalker had been freed and could go with him to Coruscant to become a Jedi. Skywalker was unsure about leaving his mother, but he always had [dreamed](/wiki/Dream "Dream") of becoming a Jedi and decided to go. After Skywalker shared a tearful goodbye with his mother, Jinn and the boy set off for the queen's ship to make their way to Coruscant.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Just before arriving at the ship, [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), a Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") and Darth Sidious' [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") attacked Jinn. The two [fought](/wiki/Duel_on_Tatooine "Duel on Tatooine") across the desert floor while Skywalker rushed back to the ship to get help, and the ship made its way to Jinn's location, where he was able to board it and flee Tatooine, leaving Darth Maul behind. Once onboard, he introduced Skywalker to Kenobi.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

With its [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") repaired, the ship finally arrived on Coruscant, where Chancellor Valorum and Senator Palpatine greeted the crew. After arriving, Jinn went before the Jedi Council and told the Jedi Masters that he believed Darth Maul was a Sith Lord. The Council was dubious of the claim, as the Order thought they [destroyed](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") the Sith a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") earlier, but they committed themselves to learn Darth Maul's identity. Jinn also revealed that he discovered Skywalker on Tatooine and believed him to be the Chosen One, asking that the boy be trained as a Jedi. At Jinn's request, the Council agreed to test Skywalker to determine if he was eligible for training. Kenobi was skeptical that Skywalker would pass the test given his age, as Jedi began their training at infancy, and worried that Jinn would defy whatever decision the Council made. Despite his Padawan's concerns, Jinn was determined to see Skywalker become a Jedi Knight.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) After the meeting, he along with [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle") met up with Dooku who offered him advice. Unbeknownst to both of them, this would be the last time they see each other.[[3]](#cite_note-The_Sith_Lord-3)

The Council tested Skywalker and agreed with Jinn that he was mighty with the Force, but declined to accept him for training. They believed that he was too old to begin training and dangerously full of fear and anger despite his power.[[6]](#cite_note-Databank-6) Nonetheless, Jinn insisted that Skywalker receive training, saying he would take the boy as his Padawan learner. Meanwhile, Kenobi could take his [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials") and become a Jedi Knight, as the Jedi Code forbade a Jedi from having two Padawans. The Council delayed the discussion for another time and ordered that Jinn and Kenobi return to Naboo as Queen Amidala was preparing to return to deal with the invasion without the [Senate's](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") help. Jinn took Skywalker with him and began giving him some initial lessons about the Force.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

#### The Duel of the Fates[]

:   "*Obi-Wan. Promise…Promise me you will train the boy.*"  
    "*Yes, Master.*"  
    "*He…*is *the Chosen One. He…*will *bring balance. Train him…*"
:   ―Jinn's dying request to Kenobi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/QuiGonDyingWish-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192810)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:QuiGonDyingWish-TPM.flac "File:QuiGonDyingWish-TPM.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

Upon arrival on Naboo, the Jedi traveled with Amidala to find the Gungans hiding in a [sacred area](/wiki/Gungan_Sacred_Place "Gungan Sacred Place") of the forests. There, the Naboo and Gungans [allied](/wiki/Boss_Meetup "Boss Meetup") to fight the Federation. The queen's handmaiden Padmé revealed herself to be the true Amidala, having masqueraded as a servant while one of her handmaidens, [Sabé](/wiki/Sab%C3%A9 "Sabé"), portrayed the queen as a safety precaution.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) Jinn, for his part, had not been fooled by the Queen's disguise since their first meeting, but had gone along with the charade for reasons of his own, which she appreciated as it helped safeguard her life.[[36]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-36) Together with the Jedi and the Gungans, Amidala put together a plan of [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), where the Gungans would fight the [Federation army](/wiki/Trade_Federation_Droid_Army "Trade Federation Droid Army") away from Theed as a diversion, allowing Amidala, her forces, and the Jedi to infiltrate the city with little opposition. Jinn made it clear, however, that while he would protect the queen, he could not fight a war for her.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

 [![Qui-Gon was outmatched by Darth Maul, leading to his demise.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/DrawCloser-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20190826010852) [![Qui-Gon was outmatched by Darth Maul, leading to his demise.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/DrawCloser-SoH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190826010852)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/DrawCloser-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20190826010852) 

Qui-Gon was outmatched by Darth Maul, leading to his demise.

 

As the [Gungan army](/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army "Gungan Grand Army") led the bulk of the Federation forces away from the city, Jinn snuck into Theed with the others and fought their way to the palace. Once in the hangar, they were again confronted by Darth Maul, who the two Jedi prepared to fight as the Naboo fought their way to the [throne](/wiki/Throne "Throne") [room](/wiki/Throne_room_(Theed_Royal_Palace) "Throne room (Theed Royal Palace)") to capture [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") Gunray. Jinn and Kenobi [fought](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") Maul in the hangar, with the Sith Lord dominating the duel, though Maul did give ground to lead the Jedi out of the hangar and throughout a [palace generator complex](/wiki/Theed_power_generator "Theed power generator"). Maul separated the two Jedi by knocking Kenobi down several levels and eventually trapping him behind shielding, leaving Jinn to fight the Sith Lord in single [combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat") without his apprentice. As they made their way through the area, the two combatants were evenly matched. However, Maul eventually countered Jinn with a physical strike from his lightsaber hilt and seized the opportunity since Jinn was off-balance, fatally stabbing the Jedi Master through the torso as Kenobi watched in horror from behind the shielding.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

When Kenobi finally reached Maul, he and the Sith Lord engaged in a furious battle, with Kenobi grieving for his master and friend. Maul was able to disarm and knock Kenobi partly down a [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") shaft and kick his lightsaber into it. Then Kenobi used the Force to summon his master's lightsaber, jump out of the pit, and slice the blade through Maul's torso in one swift movement, cutting the Sith Lord in half, sending him tumbling down the shaft,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7) and avenging Jinn.[[37]](#cite_note-SWI_230-37) Nevertheless, it was too late to save Jinn through medical intervention; no amount of [bacta](/wiki/Bacta "Bacta") could heal the maverick Jedi's mortal wound.[[38]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_AFaW-38) The Padawan ran to his dying master, cradling him in his arms, and Jinn made his apprentice promise that he would train with Skywalker as a Jedi. With his dying breath, Jinn once again said that Skywalker was the Chosen One and would bring balance to the Force.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)

### Post mortem and legacy[]

#### Effect on those he knew[]

##### Funeral and effect on the Jedi[]

:   "*The Council has granted me permission to train you. You will be a Jedi. I promise.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Anakin Skywalker, at Qui-Gon Jinn's funeral[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_I-7)
